***hurst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hurst.html>hurst</a> (38188)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hirst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wood.html>wood</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:grove.html>grove</a>; hillock; sandbank, sandbar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hyrst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hillock, eminence, <a href = vnd.unilang:height.html>height</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wood.html>wood</a>, wooded eminence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hurstiz</i>; akin <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horst.html>horst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thicket; <a href = vnd.unilang:bird.html>bird</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nest.html>nest</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:horst.html>Horst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thicket, <a href = vnd.unilang:nest.html>nest</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hurst.html>hurst</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hursts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:outside.html>outside</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:place.html>place</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:names.html>names</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wood.html>wood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grove.html>grove</a>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:huwen.html>huwen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hīwen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hīwijaną</i>.

***hypocrisie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hypocrisie.html>hypocrisie</a> (20319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ypokrosie</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:directly.html>directly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hypocrisis</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὑπόκρισις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hupókrisis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:acting.html>acting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stage.html>stage</a>, pretense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ibuprofen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ibuprofen.html>ibuprofen</a> (82620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Formed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>i</a></i><a href = vnd.unilang:so.html>so</a><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bu.html>bu</a></i>tyl<i>phen</i>yl <i><a href = vnd.unilang:pro.html>pro</a></i>pionic <a href = vnd.unilang:acid.html>acid</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ibuprofen.html>ibuprofen</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:usually.html>usually</a> uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ibuprofens</b>)
</p>
